< Review>
2 stars are for the wait.  We had reservations and were seated on time. We waited over 30 mins to order our drinks. Once we ordered our food, it took over 1 hour to be served.  The food is unique and taste good but not worth waiting for.  I did inquire  about the long wait when I  paid $$$, they said 1 cook, 1 waitresses, 1 bartender were out. They did not expect the demand for the day.  My advice call and ask them about the service wait. If you get there and are hungry you might be eating a couple of chip baskets. We were there mid week Tuesday evening.</Review>

< username>
Jennifer Quintero</username>
< rating>
5< /rating>
< Text>
Let me tell you something. Just come here. A review won't give you the entire experience of just how AMAZING the food is. Mexican seafood is normally not something I crave so when I tried this place, I didn't expect much. Now it's one of my absolute favorite places to go. My sister doesn't even like shrimp but somehow this restaurant was able to convert her.

I recommend the ceviche dishes because they are ABSOLUTELY to die for. The best ceviche I have ever had. My mouth waters just thinking about it and I wish I had more!

Spiciness Rating: Moderate-High
If you don't have a tolerance for spicy food, I'd stay away from anything that has "house spices". I LOVE spicy food and there dishes made me order multiple glasses of water. So be prepared if you want that extra kick, but it's definitely worth it! The spiciness of the food doesn't take away from the flavor!

Health Rating: Moderate-High
Most hole in the wall Mexican seafood restaurants don't have the freshest fish nor do they have many healthy options. Rest easy knowing that their seafood is fresh and you can definitely taste the quality. I recommend the octopus dishes! They also have vegan options as well so go nuts!

Atmosphere: High Quality
Stepping into the restaurant, you're greeted his with history, culture, and art at a blend of traditional and modern taste. Dining in is a must just to experience all of the beautiful Mexican art work, as well as reading the origin story of the restaurant. I could sit there forever and take in the scenery.

Service: Low-Moderate
Normally when it comes to my dinning experience, service is 50% of my interest. How often do they come check on your table, do they refill drinks, are they friendly, etc. And when it comes to service, this is the only downside to this restaurant. Whole the servers are friendly, don't expect them to be attendant. I'd expect this if a place was busy, but I have been here three separate times with varying levels or business and it's still a hassle to get their attention. There were only six tables seated and many servers but it still took multiple times to get a cup of water. Normally that's fine for me but not when my tongue is burning- While I would normally bump a star down for service, I can't do that! My heart and stomach loves the food too much to do this!

All in all, definitely try it! I BEG you to try and see for yourself!< /Text>

<Text>Such a great place and everyone especially Alex was exceptionally kind and provided the best of service.  It may seam a bit pricey at first glance but you will leave not only full but happy you tasted such well crafted food and drinks.

<text>This place has some amazing tacos! Normally when you think of tacos, you think of street tacos but this place truly elevated those $1 tacos to another level. I opted to try the of three tacos: pastor, Ensenada Style with Fish, and Volcan with pastor. All three came out nice and hot on freshly made corn tortillas. The tortillas are soft, except the Volcan, which came out on a crispy shell. Honestly, I would've ordered more and stuff my face l but since all tacos were generously portioned, I couldn't have another bite.

Another thing my friends and I enjoyed were their tortilla chips and salsa; we couldn't get enough that we asked for it twice. However, it was a bit too salty for my taste but still delicious.

I'll definitely come back for more in the future. Try this out if you're in the neighborhood or want dinner really good tacos, you won't be disappointed.<//text></record>

116369005953716583888< /UserId.>
< review>
Decent Italian food and it's a good bang for the buck. I have eaten almost all their food items except for a dish with sausages and broccoli, a meat lasagna dish, and a couple other items.
This of course has spanned about 11 years.
My first experience with Ameccis was in Fountain Valley at Magnolia and Talbert, where the first thing I tried was linguini and clams... Superb. Then I tried other items.
I was so glad to find them at a location in Irvine, as I was doing business for a few weeks there.
They are franchises and I think the consistency of quality at each franchise is remarkable.
They have a nice lunch specials, great pizza, and plenty of individual items.
Their prices have not really increased over the years, however, I do believe and I suspect the circular tins they put their food in has gotten a bit smaller. I just remember the portions weighed maybe 15% more and seemed bigger 10 years ago. It's just an observation and not really a knock because their food is so good.</review>

I attended Las Positas College in my younger years when Las Positas was just opening it's doors and I attended again and received my A.A. Degree in Liberal Arts & Sciences with an emphasis in Social Science in 2017. I was also Editor in Chief of the Las Positas College Literary Anthology. The campus is clean, the students are friendly. It's a wonderful learning environment conducive to the learning experience as a whole. The cafeteria serves great food. < Text>
The place to find unique one-off items. From clothing and accessories to furniture and trinkets. I love wandering around the aisles, getting lost and promising myself not to spend any more money. Hard to do.

They raised entrance fee prices from $3 to $5. Cash is best to have on you for most of these merchants.

Come right when it opens to find the best items. Or if you just want to browse, take your time and get here before they close or else you‚Äôll get a million reminders on the loud speaker about closing in x-amount of minutes.

There‚Äôs a cute food court area - all located out doors. Get coffees here, rest your legs and unwind.

I love how people who shop here are wearing amazing, trendy clothes.< /Text>

< Review>
Awesome market. only a cupla bucks to enter main gate.Anything and everything type traders. We found treasures! New hand painted shirts through to vintage glass! Held at Fairfax High School grounds on Melrose, only on Sunday, the area this market takes up was very worthwhile taking the time to go and wander through, as it‚Äôs extensive. If you‚Äôre looking for an ‚ÄòAladdin‚Äôs Cave‚Äô treasure hunt market, this is it. Beautiful array of stock, a visual feast, well set up alleyways. Good food available, the restrooms are in the school building, and walkways are asphalt, some shaded, some sunny. also had a beaut little mini golf area kids can use for FREE, using fancy shoes as the bumpers.<//Review>

<review>This is the place to go to in downtown when you don't know exactly what you want to eat or when you're with a lot of people and you can't decide where to eat. < Text>
What can I say,  I love the Melrose market!!!!  So many awesome vendors: clothes,  accessories,  home goods, plants, art,  vintage,  repurposed,  new,  local,  global, you name it! I've bought handmade jewelry,  rugs,  candles,  homemade beauty products etc.
We also always go to the food area and get crepes and lemonade.  They have so many choices though.  Live music as well.  The best Sunday hangout.  Entry is now $5, I seem to recall. Might want to bring cash, although most vendors do square now.< /Text>

< Text>
I could go on and on about this flea market - I have devotedly attended this Sunday tradition for years now and have watched it steadily grow in size, vendors, and popularity.  You can find an eclectic variety of wares here: vintage clothing, artisan and vintage jewelry, houseplants, antiques, local artists, new furniture from local craftsmen, food for all tastes and diets, knick-knacks galore, and even more items in between. Most vendors inside accept cash and cards, but be prepared for the cash-only entrance fee of $5. You‚Äôre guaranteed to find something you didn‚Äôt know you wanted every time you go.<//Text>

<Text>This is a relatively fun, but small flea. It carries a $5 entry, but once you're in you're greeted with mostly vintage clothes, a few succulents and/or house plants vendors, some vintage print places, local Jewelers, vintage furniture, and a pretty great coffee place. It's more of a quirky outdoor home decor shop with a cover fee, but it does have its gems. Go here for clothing, or home decor. Don't come here for bargain hunting and lots of treasure hunting.</Text>< pics>

<user>107823211788761024389< /user><username>Pauline Monk</username>< Date>
1566320143274<//Date>
<rate>4<//rate>< Review>
If you check the website, there's usually a coupon for $1 off entry.

Early bird def gets the worm here.  If you arrive early there's parking, but if you are like most of LA you aren't gonna get any parking, good luck with that!

As my friend says, it's like an outdoor goodwill, so you don't get the musty smells.  Are you spending an arm and leg on stuff you can get for a few dollars at Goodwill?  Probably!  But the goods are always unique and there are also almost always celebrities if that's your thing.

There is always awesome music in the food area.  And the food isn't bad either!  The guy in the corner doing corn bowls is awesome with delicious kombucha on tap.  Other notable eateries include the crepe place and there are always samples of fries.< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
Its a street market showcasing local artistry and people's vintage finds. What other would call junk could also be another person's treasure. No shortage of old clothes and ornaments. There's a vendor there that has a whole department store section for aloha shirts for 7.00. Great fit for summer or for a gift for your trendy teen. It's bigger than you think so take the time to explore. Also, say hi to all the dogs you'll see. Came around 1:20, didn't find parking until 2:00 so I suggest coming early. There's also a mini street market across the street. It's a great Instagram photo spot due to the fact that there's an angel wing mural at the entrance of it. Great place to visit for 2 or so hours.</review>

The hot spot for LA‚Äôs urban dwellers every Sunday, Fairfax High School parking lot is filled to the max of hipsters and kiosks ready to upscale your wardrobe or you interior decorating. Entry fee is under $5 and you can literally spend a whole day here checking out the shops, some live music and a delicious snow cone. Every trip to the Flea Market I walk away with new hand crafted jewelry or a groovy pair of sunglasses. Do yourself a favor and brave the parking to come wander around the asphalt, it will not disappoint.</Review>
